< Text>
This pizzeria is amazing! Their customer service, timing and promptness are hands down, the best in the business. The pizza is unlike others. Even the small shops. It's hardy, perfectly baked, not greasy and made to your order. I wanted extra garlic. Hell yeah, they delivered. Eat here says Dan!

Edit 17DEC20: I ordered a different pizza than I normally do. This time it was a King Arthur's Supreme, thin crust, extra sauce. The bake was spot on. Thin dough and the sauce didn't make the pizza soggy! I ordered for a future delivery time and it arrived right on time. The pizza was so hot and fresh. The quality is as consistent as In N Out, if not better. Best comfort food for these cold days and having to stay indoors. Thanks everyone at this La Mesa location!<//Text>

< review>
I have always loved Round Table, ever since my girlfriend... now wife worked there in the 80's.  It's not gourmet, but its very good, especially the pepperoni.  We recently moved into the neighborhood and visited this location for the first time yesterday.  They have a great spot in the La Mesa Springs shopping center with lots of parking, although its well within walking distance for us.

Our pizza was great... brought back lots of good memories and was just how we remembered it.  The sauce has a nice little zing to it and our pizza was piping hot when it got to the table.  Our server was pleasant and helpful.  I had a root beer because that's what you do at Round Table.  My wife had a glass of wine.   She's fancy.

This would be a 4 or 5 star review except that the restaurant was dirty.  The men's room was "deplorable" to use a current term... and the rest of the place needs a good deep cleaning.   I know its a pizza place that serves a lot of children and young people.. I understand how it got dirty... but i think they are little to comfortable leaving it that way.  I nosed around a bit, and the kitchen actually looks fine, and I will come back to this place for sure... but maybe more for take out than eat in.< /review>

<Review>Here's the thing, I was with Verizon for eons until my wife saw T-mobile's ad for an amazing veterans deal. We talked it over and went for it. We both got brand new iPhone Xrs and a nice unlimited plan.
I never once had a signal issue in all my years with Verizon, but as soon as we got rolling on the way home I went from 2 bars of LTE to 1 to 4G in the course of just driving from their store to the AG side of the Mesa. At home I get 2 bars at most and have calls drop. I can't text or even call my wife to ask her a question from inside Costco or the other stores I went to in Santa Maria the week before Thanksgiving.
With the holidays I was unable to make it back to the store before the 14 day return policy. I'm a disabled vet and don't get around as much as I'd like to be able to.
Taking my phone to Verizon I find out that T-mobile buys a model of the iPhone Xr that only has one antenna built in and cannot be used on any other carrier than AT&T after being unlocked. The other major carriers buy iPhone Xrs that have 2 antennas built in so that after paying off the phone it can be unlocked and used on any network.
Went into the store and was told it's out of their hands and to call 611 and see if they can override the 14 day policy. after 1 hour and 4 minutes being bounced between 7 different people in India, several of them told me it was up to the store I got them at, eventually I was told they would let me ship the phones back but I would still have to pay for them. (right...)
So now my wife and I have 2 3 week old iPhone Xrs which we have to pay off for $1500 and can't use them going back to Verizon. To top it all off who's going to want to buy a phone that won't work on a real network around SLO county?

I know I wont do well and will have a horrible night like this. .. why do a sleep study this way? < review>
Safe parking. Real fresh food. Real chicken light or dark meat much better than sliced sandwich meat. Fresh juice was nice. Big window view very cool. Real nice guy service. Bring cash. Vietnam, Latinos, and white people's...eat here close to Starbucks and a Vietnamese grocery store. Nail care for women men and kids right nextdoor. Interesting place.
